Everett C. Jones adjusting the educated gadget on a bathythermograph			This compact scientific mechanism, known as a bathythermograph, will be used in the National Geographic Society University of Miami research program aimed at disclosing the secrets of the ocean's strange drifting "meadows," populated by minute marine creatures known as plankton.
